Facilities: The facilities are very good. Natura bissÃ© supplies, Toto automatic toilet, Hansgrohe bridle, Dyson hair dryer, King Koil mattress. The hardware is excellent.
Environment: Near the Keyan Scenic Area, you can see the heart-shaped track under the green mountains from the window. The hotel was very considerate to help upgrade the track room. The view is very comfortable.
Service: The service is very good. There will be timely response to any needs. One good thing is that I was not asked to write a good review with my name when I checked out. Cookies were given when I checked out.
Finally, let me talk about the flaws, but I believe that as a boutique hotel, this can definitely be improved:
Hygiene: 1. The bathroom bathtub was blocked when it was drained, and it was very easy to block. You can't just rely on the knob to drain the water, you need to pull out the plug to drain the water, this needs to be noted; 2. There is no hand sanitizer/soap, which means that you have to take the shower gel in and out when washing your hands, which is not very convenient. If there is environmental protection consideration, it is recommended to place a large bottle of press-type hand sanitizer. This will be much more convenient; 3. When I went there, the soft side of the mattress was placed at the bottom, which made it very hard and painful when I slept (because I checked in because I saw the soft mattress in this hotel). In the end, I had to call the room service to turn it over in the middle of the night. This is recommended to be reminded before check-in; 4. The fluffy things on the carpet were not cleaned, which is also recommended to be improved.

But in general, the hotel is still very suitable for weekends. It is very convenient to go to Lu Town and Jianhu Lake, and the environment is pleasant. Recommended.
